			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Chipotle ANNOUNCES </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">THIRD </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">QUARTER 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;"> RESULTS</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">NEWPORT BEACH, Calif. &#x2013; October 26, 2023 &#x2013; Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) today reported financial results for its third quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font>

		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

		<p style="margin:10pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk116996176"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">"</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle&#x2019;s value proposition including customized, delicious culinary served quickly with great hospitality, is stronger than ever which is translating to great results including sustained positive transaction growth. We remain focused on developing exceptional people, preparing delicious food and fast throughput which will further strengthen our brand and continue to position us for long term growth,&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> said Brian Niccol, Chairman and CEO, Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results for the three months ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">September 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">: &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk148522998"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Total r</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">evenue in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">11.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2. The increase in total revenue was driven by new restaurant openings, and a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% increase in comparable restaurant sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">attributable to higher transactions and, to a lesser extent, an increase in average check</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> Digital sales represented 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% of total food and beverage revenue.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">62 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">new restaurants during the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">with 54 locations </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">including a Chipotlane. These formats continue to perform well and are helping enhance guest access and convenience, as well as increase new restaurant sa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">les, margins, and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">returns. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs in the third quarter were 29.7% of total revenue, a decrease of about 10 basis points compared to the third quarter of 2022. Th</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">e benefit from last year&#x2019;s menu price increases </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> mostly offset by inflation across several food costs, primarily beef and queso.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in the third quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">was 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">compared to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">25.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">improvement was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to the benefit of sales leverage</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> partially offset by higher inflation across several food costs and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> to a lesser extent, wage inflation.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>

		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter were $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">159.5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> on a GAAP basis, or $158.2 million on a non-GAAP basis, excluding $1.3 million of corporate restructuring costs related to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">May 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> optimization of our organizational structure</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the third quarter also include $119.3 million of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">underlying general and administrative expenses</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">34.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million of non-cash stock compensation</font><a name="_Hlk100747727"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, $3.4 million of higher performance-based accruals and payroll taxes on equity vesting and exercises and $1.2 million of other costs, primarily related to our upcoming All Managers Conference scheduled for the first quarter of 2024. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The effective income tax rate for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was 24.2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> compared to 24.4% in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><a name="_Hlk116971941"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2. The decrease in the effective income tax rate was</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">primarily due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">a decrease in uncertain tax position reserves and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher income tax credits, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">mostly</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> offset by a decrease in tax benefits from option exercises and equity vesting</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk132644374"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">313.2 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">million, or $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">11.32</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">compared to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">257.1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9.20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">In the third quarter of 2023, e</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">xcluding the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> $0.04 after-tax impact from expenses related to corporate restructuring, adjusted diluted earnings per share was $11.36. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">During the&nbsp;third quarter, our Board of Directors approved the investment of up to an additional $300 million, exclusive of commissions, to repurchase shares of our common stock, subject to market conditions. Including this repurchase authorization, $368.4&nbsp;million was available as of September 30, 2023. The repurchase authorization may be modified, suspended, or discontinued at any time. We repurchased $226.3&nbsp;million of stock at an average price per share of $1,913.98&nbsp;during the third quarter.</font>
		</p>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3,300</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">September 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> in North America and Europe</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 2023 list for Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies and Time Magazine&#x2019;s Most Influential Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">110</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements</font>

We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;may&#x201D;, &#x201C;approximately&#x201D;, &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: increasing wage inflation and the competitive labor market,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">including as a result of regulations such as California AB 1228,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> which impacts our ability to attract and retain qualified employees and has resulted in occasional staffing shortages; the impact of any union organizing efforts and our responses to such efforts; increasing supply costs (including beef, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">tortillas, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">queso</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">, salsa, beans and rice</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">); risks of food safety incidents and food-borne illnesses; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential material failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">including risk of breaches, unauthorized access, theft, modification or destruction of guest or employee personal or confidential information stored on our network or the network of third party providers</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the financial impact of increasing our average hourly wages; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> costs and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> availability of suitable new restaurant sites</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">construction materials and contractors</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">and the expected costs to accelerate our international expansion through franchise restaurants in the Middle East</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">to inflation, global conflicts, climate change, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">our Food </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">ith Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased consumer spending (including as a result of higher inflation, mass layoffs, fear of possible recession and higher energy prices), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">and potentially class action litigation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">related to food safety incidents</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">, cybersecurity incidents,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> employment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> or privacy</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> laws, advertising claims or other matters; 		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">CHIPOTLE MEXICAN GRILL, INC.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant and corporate asset impairment, corporate restructuring, certain legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, unrealized gains on equity investments, separation costs, and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding corporate restructuring, certain legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, separation costs, and certain other costs. The adjusted effective income tax rate is the effective income tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, adjusted effective income tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>
